                            <a href="Latest-News" target="_blank">
                                <h1 style="font-size: 24px;">The Face of Real Estate Property  in Mumbai</h1>
                            </a>
                            <div class="vticker" style="position:relative">
                                <p>Owning a property anywhere in India is a big deal-thanks to the sky rocketing property prices. Whether you are planning to buy a small studio apartment or a lavish 3BHK flat, the rate of property per square inch has gone up in the last ten years. Metropolitan cities like Delhi, Bangalore and Mumbai have seen most of the hike. While being one of the most expensive cities to invest in real estate, Mumbaiis also one of the best cities investments per se. With sprawling entertainment centres, magnificent sea facing areas and the ever-glitzy Bollywood industry, the city has a charm of its own. All these factors have led to the rise of expensive <a style="font-weight: bold; cursor: pointer" href="http://www.hindustanproperty.com/real-estate-property-in-Mumbai">Real Estate in Mumbai</a>.</p><p>While the city has expanded to both urban and suburban limits, some prime areas remain an all-time favourite when investing in <a style="font-weight: bold; cursor: pointer" href="http://www.hindustanproperty.com/real-estate-property-in-Mumbai">Real Estate in Mumbai</a> is being considered. Dadar is one such place in Mumbai that is a favourite among property seekers. The area, especially Shivaji Park is known for its old world charm coupled with modern outlook the localities hold. With many corporate jobs being created near the heart of the city, seeking a<a style="font-weight: bold; cursor: pointer" href="http://www.hindustanproperty.com/real-estate-property-in-Mumbai"> property for Sale in Mumbai</a> in the Dadar area can be quite a fussy yet satisfying act if you could get your hands on a good property. The area is marked with three prominent cinema halls, many entertainment hubs, the beautiful beach at Dadar Chowpatty and the famous Siddhivinayak temple.</p><p>Another noteworthy area preferred by many when looking for <a style="font-weight: bold; cursor: pointer" href="http://www.hindustanproperty.com/real-estate-property-in-Mumbai">Property in Mumbai</a> is Andheri. It is one of the most posh localities of Mumbai, lined up by a number of shopping centres, restaurants, multiplexes and the citys international airport, the Chhatrapai Shivaji International Airport. The locality boasts a healthy mix of residential and commercial areas. Many <a style="font-weight: bold; cursor: pointer" href="http://www.hindustanproperty.com/real-estate-property-in-Mumbai">new projects in Mumbai </a>are coming up in this area that range around the price range of INR 2 crores and above. A <a style="font-weight: bold; cursor: pointer" href="http://www.hindustanproperty.com/real-estate-property-in-Mumbai">2BHK flat in Mumbai</a> could cost you anywhere around INR 2-2.5 crore in this localitydepending upon the area of the flats and the amenities offered.  Andheri is, in fact, one of the biggest inhabited suburbs of Mumbai.</p><p>Other areas such as Worli and Lower Parel offer great <a style="font-weight: bold; cursor: pointer">new projects in Mumbai </a>where investment in Real Estate can be considered. These areas are now bustling with people of all strata. Both the localities have a great mix of commercial and residential properties. If you are looking for <a style="font-weight: bold; cursor: pointer" href="http://www.hindustanproperty.com/real-estate-property-in-Mumbai">property in Navi Mumbai,</a> Thane, Panvel, Vashi and Kamothe are the localities to look for. Many new as well as renowned builders are coming up with <a style="font-weight: bold; cursor: pointer" href="http://www.hindustanproperty.com/real-estate-property-in-Mumbai">2BHK flats in Mumbai</a> in these rates at affordable rates.</p><p>Apart from looking for preferable locations for <a style="font-weight: bold; cursor: pointer" href="http://www.hindustanproperty.com/real-estate-property-in-Mumbai">property in Mumbai</a>, it is essential to consider certain factors while investing in <a style="font-weight: bold; cursor: pointer" href="http://www.hindustanproperty.com/real-estate-property-in-Mumbai">Real Estate in Mumbai.</a> An easy way to not fall into the incentive pitfalls is to remind yourself that you are investing. Always look for long-term gains rather than short-term incentives offered by builders offering <a style="font-weight: bold; cursor: pointer" href="http://www.hindustanproperty.com/real-estate-property-in-Mumbai">Property for Sale in Mumbai.</a> Before making any investment decision, always be aware of the going rate and analyse the state of market. A <a style="font-weight: bold; cursor: pointer" href="http://www.hindustanproperty.com/real-estate-property-in-Mumbai">Property in Navi Mumbai</a> can be well within your budget if you do a thorough research regarding the on-going real estate trend in the area. Also, remember to compute your rental yield in case you are planning to put the property on rent. Always learn to prioritize the location over the size of the property or the amenities offered by the builder. Keeping these factors in mind can yield you a good <a style="font-weight: bold; cursor: pointer">property in Mumbai.</a></p>
                            </div>

    <script>
        function FillData(ProjectId, id) {
            $("#txtProjectid").text(ProjectId);
            CleareBeforLoad();
            if (id == 1) {
                
                $("#contact").show();
                $("#Details").hide();
                $(".MainHeading").text("Contact Advertiser");
                $("#message1").text("Thanks for Contact Us for this Project.");
                $("#message2").text("We will get in touch with you");
                $("#message3").text("soon with more details.");
                $("#header").text("Contact us for complete details of this Excellent Project");
                ShowDialog(true);
                e.preventDefault();

            }
            else {
                $("#contact").show();
                $("#Details").hide();
                $(".MainHeading").text("Contact Advertiser");
                $("#message1").text("Thanks for showing your interest in this Project. ");
                $("#message2").text("We will get in touch with you soon");
                $("#message3").text("with more details.");
                $("#header").text("Interested in the Project? Please fill in your details below ");
                ShowDialog(true);
                e.preventDefault();
            }

        }

        function CleareBeforLoad()
        {
            $("#ContentPlaceHolder1_TextBox1").val("");
            $("#ContentPlaceHolder1_txtMobileNo").val("");
            $("#ContentPlaceHolder1_TextBox2").val("");
            $("#ContentPlaceHolder1_Textarea1").val("");
            $("#ContentPlaceHolder1_Textarea1").css({ 'border-color': '' });
            $("#ContentPlaceHolder1_lblErrorName").text("");
            $("#ContentPlaceHolder1_TextBox1").css({ 'border-color': '' });
            $("#ContentPlaceHolder1_lblErrorEmail").text("");
            $("#ContentPlaceHolder1_TextBox2").css({ 'border-color': '' });
            $("#ContentPlaceHolder1_lblErrorMobileNo").text("");
            $("#ContentPlaceHolder1_txtMobileNo").css({ 'border-color': '' });
        }



        function disableIfLogin() {

            $('#ContentPlaceHolder1_txtName').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
            $('#ContentPlaceHolder1_txtEmail').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
            $('#ContentPlaceHolder1_txtMobile').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
        }

        function ShowDetail() {
            $("#divDetail").show();
        }

        function HideDetails() {
            $("#divDetail").hide();
        }

        function hoverdiv(location, builderName, Area, Propertycost, id, PropertyDesc) {
            var builder = builderName;
            var area = Area;
            var cost = Propertycost;
            $(".balon").css({ "overflow": "visible" });
            $("#" + id).balloon({
                //offsetX: 0,
                //offsetY: 0,
                tipSize: 24,
                css: {
                    border: 'solid 4px #5baec0',
                    backgroundColor: 'white',
                    opacity: 1,
                    delay: 5,
                    position: 'left',
                    overflow: 'visible',
                    overflowX: 'visible',
                    overflowY: 'visible',
                    color: 'black'
                },
                contents: '<span>' + PropertyDesc + '</span><br/>' +
                          '<span><strong>Builder Name: </strong>' + builder + '</span><br/>' +
                          '<span><strong>Area: </strong>' + area + ' sq.ft.</span><br/>' +
                          '<span><strong>Cost: </strong>Rs ' + cost + '</span><br/>'
               
            });
        }

        function hoverdivAgentImg(location, AgentName, FirnName, Dealing, id) {

            $("#" + id).balloon({
                offsetX: 0,
                offsetY: 0,
                tipSize: 24,
                css: {
                    border: 'solid 4px #5baec0',
                    backgroundColor: 'white',
                    opacity: 1,
                    color: 'black'
                },
                contents: '<span><strong>Agent Name: </strong>' + AgentName + '</span><br/>' +
                          '<span><strong>Firm Name: </strong>' + FirnName + '</span><br/>' +
                          '<span><strong>Location: </strong>' + location + '</span><br/>' +
                          '<span><strong>Dealing In: </strong>' + Dealing + '</span><br/>'

            });
        }


        


    </script>

      $(document).ready(function () {
          // Remove style
         
          // All city End

          // Mobile Search 
          if ($(window).width() > 1024) {
              //desktop
          } else {
              

              // Hack Code Start
              $(document).on('touchstart', 'div[search-mobile]', function (e) {
                  $("html").css({ "overflow": "hidden" });
                  $("body").toggleClass("mobileSearch");
                 // $("#ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolder1_txtLocationMob").focus();
                  //console.log("search-mobile");
              });
              $(document).on('touchstart', '.m-search-overlay', function (e) {
                  $("html").removeAttr("style");
                  $("body").toggleClass("mobileSearch");
                  //console.log("overlay");
              });
              $(document).on('touchstart', '.view-details-btn', function (event) {
                  event.preventDefault();
                  window.open($(this).attr("href"), '_blank');
              });

          };

      });
</script>
    <script>

        function ValidateEmail(email) {
            var expr = /^([\w-\.]+)@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.)|(([\w-]+\.)+))([a-zA-Z]{2,4}|[0-9]{1,3})(\]?)$/;
            return expr.test(email);
        };

    </script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
            $(document).ready(function () {

                $("#btnCloseSub").click(function (e) {
                    HideSubDialog();
                    e.preventDefault();

                });

                $("#overlay").click(function (e) {
                    HideSubDialog();
                });

                    if (event.keyCode == 13) {

                        event.preventDefault();
                    }
                });

            });

            $(document).keyup(function (e) {

                if (e.keyCode == 27) {
                    HideSubDialog();
                }   // escape key maps to keycode `27`
            });
            function ShowSubDialog(modal) {
                $("#divaskOverlay").show();
                $("#dialogSub").fadeIn(300);

                if (modal) {
                    $("#divaskOverlay").bind("click");
                }
                else {
                    $("#divaskOverlay").click(function (e) {
                        HideSubDialog();
                    });
                }
            }

            function HideSubDialog() {
                $("#divaskOverlay").hide();
                $("#dialogSub").fadeOut(300);
            }
        </script>

        <script>

            function CheckAndOpen() {
                var usercode = '';
                //alert(usercode);
                if (usercode == "") {
                    //data-toggle="modal" data-target="#signin"
                    //$("#postproperty").attr("data-toggle", "modal");
                    //$("#postproperty").attr("data-target", "#signin");
                    ShowSignIn();
                }
                else {
                    $("#postproperty").attr("href", "Post-Your-Property");
                }
            }

            function ValidateEmail(email) {
                var expr = /^([\w-\.]+)@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.)|(([\w-]+\.)+))([a-zA-Z]{2,4}|[0-9]{1,3})(\]?)$/;
                return expr.test(email);
            }

            $(document).ready(function () {

                $("#Submit").click(function (e) {
                    
                    var expr = /^([\w-\.]+)@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.)|(([\w-]+\.)+))([a-zA-Z]{2,4}|[0-9]{1,3})(\]?)$/;
                    if ($("#txtEmail").val() != "") {
                        if (!expr.test($("#txtEmail").val())) {
                            $("#txtEmail").css({ "border-color": "red" });
                            $("#lblEmailerror").text("Please Enter valid email");
                            return false;
                        }
                        else {
                            ShowSubDialog(true);
                            var param = {
                                EmailId: $("#txtEmail").val()
                            };

                            $.ajax({

                                url: "DefaultOld.aspx/InsertSubscription",

                                data: JSON.stringify(param),

                                dataType: "json",

                                type: "POST",

                                contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",

                                dataFilter: function (data) { return data; },

                                success: function (data) {
                                    if (data.d != "") {
                                        //alert('1');
                                        $("#txtEmail").css({ "border-color": "red" });
                                        //ShowSubDialog(true);
                                        //$("#lblEmailerror").text("Email Id Already Subscribed");
                                        $("#Span1").text('Email Id already subscribed');
                                        $("#Subthank").text('');
                                    }
                                    else {
                                        //alert('2');
                                        $("#txtEmail").css({ "border-color": "" });
                                        $("#lblEmailerror").text("");
                                        $("#Span1").text('Your Subscription is submitted successfully. You will soon receive revert from hindustanproperty.com');
                                        $("#txtEmail").val("");
                                    }
                                }
                            });
                            return false;
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        $("#txtEmail").css({ "border-color": "red" });
                        $("#lblEmailerror").text("Please Enter Email Id");
                        return false;
                    }
                });


                $("#txtEmail").blur(function () {
                    var expr = /^([\w-\.]+)@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.)|(([\w-]+\.)+))([a-zA-Z]{2,4}|[0-9]{1,3})(\]?)$/;
                    if ($("#txtEmail").val() == "") {
                        $("#txtEmail").css({ "border-color": "red" });
                        $("#lblEmailerror").text("Please Enter Email Id");
                    }
                    else {
                        $("#txtEmail").css({ "border-color": "" });
                        $("#lblEmailerror").text("");
                    }
                    if ($("#txtEmail").val() != "") {
                        if (!expr.test($("#txtEmail").val())) {
                            $("#txtEmail").css({ "border-color": "red" });
                            $("#lblEmailerror").text("Please Enter valid email");
                            return false;
                        }
                        else {
                            $("#txtEmail").css({ "border-color": "" });
                            $("#lblEmailerror").text("");
                            return true;
                        }
                    }

                });

            });

        </script>

        <script>
            function ShowSignIn()
            {
                var usercode = ''
                if (usercode.length > 0) {
                   
                }
                else {
                    $("#RegisPop").modal();
                    $("#signup").css("display", "none");
                    $("#VerificationMaster").css("display", "none");
                    $("#DivRegSucsses").css("display", "none");
                    $("#DivForgotMail").css("display", "none");
                    $("#signin").css("display", "block");
                    $("#DivVerification").css("display", "none");
                    CleareSignIn();
                }
            }
            function ShowSignUp() {
                $("#RegisPop").modal();
                $("#signup").css("display", "block");
                $("#VerificationMaster").css("display", "none");
                $("#DivRegSucsses").css("display", "none");
                $("#DivForgotMail").css("display", "none");
                $("#signin").css("display", "none");
                CleareControls();

            }
            function ShowVerification() {
                $("#RegisPop").modal();
                $("#signup").css("display", "none");
                $("#VerificationMaster").css("display", "block");
                $("#DivRegSucsses").css("display", "none");
                $("#DivForgotMail").css("display", "none");
                $("#signin").css("display", "none");

            }
            function ShowRegSucc() {
                $("#RegisPop").modal();
                $("#signup").css("display", "none");
                $("#VerificationMaster").css("display", "none");
                $("#DivRegSucsses").css("display", "block");
                $("#DivForgotMail").css("display", "none");
                $("#signin").css("display", "none");

            }
            function ShowForgetMail() {
                $("#RegisPop").modal();
                $("#signup").css("display", "none");
                $("#VerificationMaster").css("display", "none");
                $("#DivRegSucsses").css("display", "none");
                $("#DivForgotMail").css("display", "block");
                $("#signin").css("display", "none");

            }

            function CleareControls()
            {
                $("#txtUserName").css('border-color', '');
                $("#txtUserName").val("");
                $("#lbluserName").text("");

                $("#txtEmail1").css('border-color', '');
                $("#txtEmail1").val("");
                $("#lblErroeEmail1").text("");

                $("#txtMobileNo").css('border-color', '');
                $("#txtMobileNo").val("");
                $("#lblmobileno").text("");

                $("#txtPassword").css('border-color', '');
                $("#txtPassword").val("");
                $("#lblerrorpassword").text("");

                $("#txtConfirmPass").css('border-color', '');
                $("#txtConfirmPass").val("");
                $("#lblerrorcpwd").text("");
            }

            function CleareSignIn()
            {
                $("#txtLoginUserName").css('border-color', '');
                $("#txtLoginUserName").val("");
                $("#lblLoginUserError").text("");

                $("#txtLogPassword").css('border-color', '');
                $("#txtLogPassword").val("");
                $("#lblLoginPasswordError").text("");
                $("#lblLoginError").text("");
            }
        </script>
